In [8]:
 
for p in paths:
    if p['id']:
        count = datadict[p['id']]
    if count >=39 :
        color_class =5
    elif count >=37:
        color_class =4
    elif count >=35:
        color_class =3
    elif count >=33:
        color_class =2
    elif count >=31:
        color_class =1
    else :
        color_class =0
    color = colors[color_class]
    p['fill'] = color
